route-policy rpToBR
  if destination in plDefaultRoute then
    set med 10000
    set next-hop self
    pass
  elseif destination in plTo163 then
    drop
  elseif as-path in (ios-regex '^$') then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy rpToCR
  if destination in plTo163 then
    drop
  elseif destination in plTo163new then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy rpToSR
  if destination in plDefaultRoute then
    set med 10000
    pass
  elseif tag eq 100 then
    pass
  else
